Ubuntu Mono Regular (UbuntuMono-Regular.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

If NID 2 and 17 = 'Regular': Mac NID 16 should match NID 1.
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). This is true for MS Office Version 1639 and lower. Even though Microsoft has changed it with version 1640 (fast insider, June 2020) we keep this as an error, because most of the current MS Office users won't update in the near future. More infos here:
Cross Platform Issues

MS NID 16/17

If NID 2 and 17 = 'Regular': MS NID 16 should match NID 1.
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). This is true for MS Office Version 1639 and lower. Even though Microsoft has changed it with version 1640 (fast insider, June 2020) we keep this as an error, because most of the current MS Office users won't update in the near future. More infos here:
Cross Platform Issues

NID 16 'Ubuntu Mono' = NID 1 'Ubuntu Mono'.

Pass

Ubuntu Mono Italic (UbuntuMono-Italic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'UbuntuMono-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Ubuntu Mono Italic (UbuntuMono-Italic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
'space' in NID 6 cause issues in fontbook for Mac.

NID 6 is 'UbuntuMono-Italic', Everything looks good.

Ubuntu Mono Italic (UbuntuMono-Italic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

Mac NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Ubuntu Mono' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Italic' = NID 1 'Ubuntu Mono' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Pass

Ubuntu Mono Italic (UbuntuMono-Italic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'UbuntuMono-Italic', Everything looks good.

Ubuntu Mono Italic (UbuntuMono-Italic.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Ubuntu Mono' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Italic' = NID 1 'Ubuntu Mono' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Pass

Ubuntu Mono Bold Italic (UbuntuMono-BoldItalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'UbuntuMono-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Ubuntu Mono Bold Italic (UbuntuMono-BoldItalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 16/17

Mac NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Ubuntu Mono' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Bold Italic' = NID 1 'Ubuntu Mono' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Bold Italic'.

Pass

gasp Table

gasp Table

Error

Ubuntu Mono Regular (UbuntuMono-Regular.ttf)

gasp

Version

gasp table verison should be 1.

Verison = 0

Info

Ubuntu Mono Regular (UbuntuMono-Regular.ttf)

gasp

Default

Pull gasp table Default.

Do gray = True

Warning

Ubuntu Mono Regular (UbuntuMono-Regular.ttf)

gasp

Default

Check gasp table Default.

gasp table default is:
Do gray = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

Error

Ubuntu Mono Italic (UbuntuMono-Italic.ttf)

gasp

PostScript names

Every PostScript name is fine.
